Jamison Brereton

35 (655)
As╠Бvins
┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼Ыva ─Аtreya
24 verses: pariс╣гс╣н─Бjjyotis, except paс╣Еkti 22, 24 and mah─Бbr╠еhat─л 24, arranged in trcas. ╠е
The Anukramaс╣З─лтАЩs attribution of this hymn to ┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼Ыva is supported by his self-refer ence in verses 19тАУ21 and his reference to his ancestor Atri in verse 19, but the virtuos ity so characteristic of ┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼ЫvaтАЩs Marut hymns in Maс╣Зс╕Нala V is not on display here. This long hymn may be one of the most repetitive in the R╠еgveda. In the first twenty one verses the c-p─Бda is identical, and the tr╠еcas making up the hymn all have refrains encompassing at least the second half-verse (p─Бdas cd: vss. 1тАУ3; p─Бdas cde: vss. 22тАУ24) and usually the second (b) p─Бda as well (bcd: vss. 4тАУ6, 7тАУ9, 10тАУ12, 13тАУ15, 16тАУ18, 19тАУ21). This leaves the first (a) p─Бda as the only locus of variation in each tr╠еca, and even that variation is patterned and under strict control. Moreover, the contents and phraseology of the individual tr╠еcas do not differ significantly one from anotherтАФurg ing the A┼Ыvins to come to the sacrifice with numerous other gods and to partake of our offerings while providing us with gifts and aid in return. The repetitive structure has an incantatory effect, but it does not challenge the decoding skills of the audience.
The most interesting tr╠еca consists of verses 16тАУ18. As a number of others have pointed out, these three verses, asking the A┼Ыvins to тАЬquickenтАЭ or тАЬanimateтАЭ various things for us, are appropriate to the three varс╣Зas in turn: verse 16 to the brahmin, 17 to the kс╣гatriya, and 18 to the vai┼Ыya. In fact, verse 16 begins with the word bra╠Бhma, while 17 begins with kс╣гatra╠Бm. In 16 we ask for the A┼ЫvinsтАЩ aid for ritual and priestly elements, in 17 for elements related to kingly and martial power, and in 18 for our livestock and people. As is well known, the varс╣Зa system is not a prominent feature of the R╠еgveda and may well only be taking shape in this period, but this small collec tion of ┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼Ыva hymns displays it clearlyтАФnot only in this tr╠еca, but in the next two twinned hymns (36 and 37) with their reference to bra╠Бhman and kс╣гatra╠Б respectively.

Jamison Brereton Notes

A┼Ыvins See the published introduction. for the pattern of repetitions in this very repetitious hymn.

The c p─Бda of every vs. save for the last three (22-24), тАЬin concert with Dawn and the SunтАЭ (saj├│с╣гas─Б uс╣г├бs─Б s┼л╠Бryeс╣Зa ca), of course refers to the A┼ЫvinsтАЩ participation in the dawn sacrifice.

Griffith

WITH Agni and with Indra, Visnu. Varuna, with the Adityas, Rudras, Vasus, closely leagued;
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, O Asvins, drink the Soma juice.

English translation:

тАЬPowerful (A┼Ыvins), associated with all intelligences, with all beings, with heaven, with earth, with themountains, united with the dawn and with the S┼лrya, drink, A┼Ыvins, the Soma.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

With all insights and (all) creation, o prizewinners, in comradeship with Heaven and Earth and the stones,
in concert with Dawn and the Sun, drink the soma, o A┼Ыvins.

Griffith

With all the Holy Thoughts, all being Mighty Ones! in close alliance wil the Mountains, Heaven, and Earth;
Accordant. of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, O Asvins, drink the Soma juice.

Grassmann

Mit allen Geistern, mit der Welt, o reiche ihr, mit Erd’ und Himmel, mit den Felsen im Verein, Mit Morgenroth und Sonne in Gemeinschaft trinkt, o Ritter, ihr, den Somatrank.

Elizarenkova

English translation:

тАЬBe gratified by our praise as youths are delighted (by the voices) of maidens; recognize, deities, all theofferings in this ceremony; united with the dawn adn with S┼лrya, bring us, A┼Ыvins, food.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Enjoy the praise song, like youths a maiden. тАУ Come down here to all our pressings, o gods.
In concert with Dawn and the Sun, convey refreshment to us, o A┼Ыvins.

Griffith

Accept our praise-song as a youth accepts a maid. Come nigh, O ye Twain Gods, to all libations here.
Accordant, of one mind with Sarya and with Dawn O Asvins, bring us strengthening food.

Geldner

Habt Wohlgefallen an dem Lobliede wie J├╝nglinge an einer Jungfrau, findet euch, beide G├╢tter, bei allen Trinkopfern hier ein, eintr├дchtig mit Usas und Surya bringt uns Labsal, o Asvin.

Grassmann

Geniesst das Opfer, wie der J├╝ngling M├дdchen k├╝sst, zu allen Spenden kommt, o G├╢tter, hier herab, Und mit der Sonn’ und Morgenr├╢the im Verein, o Ritter, fahrt uns Labung zu.

Elizarenkova

тАЬYou alight upon the effused Soma as the H─Бridrav─Б plural nges unto the water; you fall upon it like twobuffaloes (plural nging into a pool); united with the dawn and with S┼лrya, come, A┼Ыvins, by the triple path.тАЭ

H─Бridrav─Б: a tree; by the triple path: trir vartir y─Бtam, the three daily ceremonies; or, come thrice to ourdwelling

Jamison Brereton

Like h─Бridrava-birds (to the woods), you fly right to the wooden (cups). тАУ Like buffaloes (to water), you come down to the
pressed soma.
In concert with Dawn and the Sun, drive your circuit three times, o A┼Ыvins.

Ye fly as starlings fly unto the forest trees; like buffaloes ye seek the Soma we have shed.
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, come thrice, O Asvins, to our home.

English translation:

тАЬAs two geese, as two travellers, as two buffaloes (hasten to water), you alight, A┼Ыvins, upon the effusedSoma; united with the dawn and with S┼лrya, come, A┼Ыvins, by the triple path.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Like geese you fly, like travelers on the road. тАУ Like buffaloes (to water), you come down to the pressed soma.
In concert with Dawn and the Sun, drive your circuit three times, o A┼Ыvins.

Griffith

Ye fly like swans, like those who travel on their way; like buffaloes ye seek the Soma we have shed.
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, come thrice, O Asvins, to our home.

Geldner

Wie G├дnse flieget ihr, wie Wanderer eilet ihr, ihr findet euch, beide G├╢tter, bei allen Trinkopfern hier ein, eintr├дchtig mit Usas und Surya bringt uns Labsal, o Asvin.

Wie Schw├дne und wie Wanderv├╢gel flieget ihr, wie B├╝ffel kommt ihr zum gepressten Soma her, Und mit der Sonn’ und Morgenr├╢the im Verein, kommt, Ritter, dreimal in den Hof.

English translation:

тАЬYou hasten like two falcons to the offerer of the libation, you alight upon the effused Soma as twobuffaloes (hasten to water), united with the dawn and with S┼лrya, come, A┼Ыvins, by the triple path.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Like falcons you fly to the distribution of oblations. тАУ Like buffaloes (to water), you come down to the pressed soma.
In concert with Dawn and the Sun, drive your circuit three times, o A┼Ыvins.

Griffith

Ye fly to our oblation like a pair of hawks; like buffaloes ye seek the Soma we have shed.
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, come thrice, O Asvins, to our home.

Griffith

Come hitherward and drink and satisfy yourselves, bestow upon us progeny and affluence.
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, O Asvins, grant us vigorous strength.

English translation:

тАЬConquer (A┼Ыvins), your foes; protect and praise (your worshipper), grant progeny, give wealth, andunited with the dawn and with S┼лrya, give us, A┼Ыvins, strength.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Conquer and sing praise and offer help. тАУ Provide progeny and provide property.
In concert with Dawn and the Sun, provide nourishment for us, o A┼Ыvins.

Jamison Brereton Notes

The distribution of caтАЩs in p─Бda a is somewhat puzzling or, perhaps, syncopated, with the 2nd ca following preverb+verb (pr├б stutaс╣Г ca), though the other two preverb/verb combinations in this tс╣Ыca place the ca in the expected position after the preverb (─Б╠Бca gachatam 10a and immediately following pr├б c─Бvatam 11a). This does not seem to be metri causa, or at least not in some obvious way.

Jamison Brereton Notes

The first hemistichs of the three verses in this tс╣Ыca are excessively provided with caтАЩs, as well as 2nd du. act. impvs in -tam. Cf., e.g., 10ab p├нbataс╣Г ca tс╣Ыpс╣Зut├бс╣Г c─Б╠Бca gachatam, praj─Б╠Бс╣Г ca dhatt├бm dr├бviс╣Зaс╣Г ca dhattam.

Griffith

Conquer your foes, protect us, praise your worshippers; bestow upon us progeny and affluence.
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, O Asvins, grant us vigolms strength.

Geldner

Sieget und stimmet das Lob an und helfet weiter und bringet Kinder und bringet Reichtum, eintr├дchtig mit Usas und Surya, bringet uns Kraft, o Asvin!

English translation:

тАЬAssociated with Mitra and Varuс╣Зa, with Dharma, with the Maruts, repair to the invocation of the adorer;repair (to him), A┼Ыvins, united with the dawn, with S┼лrya and with the ─Аdityas.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Accompanied by Mitra and Varuс╣Зa and accompanied by their statute, accompanied by the Maruts you go to the singerтАЩs call.
тАУ In concert with Dawn and the Sun, drive with the ─Аdityas, o A┼Ыvins.

Jamison Brereton Notes

Exactly what dh├бrmavant- is conveying here is unclear, but it is highly unlikely to be, with Geldner, тАЬvon Dharma [den Gesetz] тАж begleitet,тАЭ since тАШlawтАЩ is quite anachronistic for dh├бrma(n)-. I also do not think Renou is correct in seeing it as a proper noun, despite its appearance in a -vant-stem parallel to those containing godsтАЩ names.

Rather, the repetitive template of the tс╣Ыca imposes the -vant-stem here, on the abstract principle dh├бrman- generally associated with Mitra and Varuс╣Зa – here perhaps referring to their authority and its manifestation (their statute) by which they impose order on the world.

Griffith

With Mitra, Varuna, Dharma, and the Maruts in your company approach unto your praiser’s call.
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, and with the Adityas, Asvins! come.

Geldner

Von Mitra und Varuna, und von Dharma, dem Gesetz, von den Marut begleitet kommet ihr auf des S├дngers Ruf, eintr├дchtig mit Usas und Surya, mit den Aditya┬┤s kommet, o Asvin!

Grassmann

Vereint mit Mitra-Varuna und dem Gesetz und mit den Maruts kommt ihr zu des S├дngers Ruf, Vereinigt mit der Sonne und dem Morgenroth und den Aditja’s, Ritter, kommt.

Elizarenkova

Griffith

Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, and with the Adityas, Asvins! come.

Jamison Brereton Notes

A verb needs to be supplied with the d p─Бdas of this tс╣Ыca (s├│maс╣Г sunvat├│ a┼Ыvin─Б). On both general grounds and the d p─Бdas of vss. 1-3 (s├│mam pibatam a┼Ыvin─Б)(see also 22b p├нbatam somy├бm m├бdhu), тАШdrinkтАЩ makes the most sense, though тАШdrive toтАЩ, which dominates the middle part of the hymn, is certainly possible.

A verb needs to be supplied with the d p─Бdas of this tс╣Ыca (s├│maс╣Г sunvat├│ a┼Ыvin─Б). On both general grounds and the d p─Бdas of vss. 1-3 (s├│mam pibatam a┼Ыvin─Б)(see also 22b p├нbatam somy├бm m├бdhu), тАШdrinkтАЩ makes the most sense, though тАШdrive toтАЩ, which dominates the middle part of the hymn, is certainly possible.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬHumblers of the pride (of your enemies), hear the earnest praise of ┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼Ыva offering libations as(you did) that of Atri, and, united with the dawn and with S┼лrya, (drink), A┼Ыvins, (the Soma) prepared theprevious day.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Soma prepared the previous day: tiro ahnyam = Soma prepared the day before, and drunk at earlydaawn, at the worship of the A┼Ыvins

Jamison Brereton

As if to AtriтАЩs, listen to the first praise hymn of the presser ┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼Ыva, o you roused to exuberance.
тАУ In concert with Dawn and the Sun, o A┼Ыvins, (drink) the (soma) aged overnight.

Griffith

As ye heard Atri’s earliest eulogy, so hear Syavasva, Soma-presser, ye who reel in joy.
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, drink juice, O Asvins, three days old.

Geldner

H├╢ret wie auf des Atri so auf des somapressenden Syavasva Erstlob, ihr Rauscherregten! Eintr├дchtig mit Usas und Surya trinket den gestrigen Soma, o Asvin!

Grassmann

Wie einst des Atri h├╢rt das erste sch├╢nste Lob des Somapressers ├Зj─Бvaa├зva, trunkerregt, Vereinigt mit der Sonne und dem Morgenroth, trinkt, Ritter, den gegorenen.

Elizarenkova

Further like running streams Syavasva’s eulogies who presses out the Soma, ye who reel in joy.

English translation:

тАЬCome, leaders of rites, when the sacrifice, at which your adoration is cited, is commenced, to drink ofthe Soma offered by me; come, A┼Ыvins, come (here), desirous of protection, I invoke you; give precious riches tothe donor of the offering.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Offered by me: vivakс╣гaс╣Зasya is an epithet of the speaker, i.e., at the commencementadoration of me the offerer of libation; or, it is an epithet of the Soma, heaven-bestowing, svargapr─Бpaс╣Зa┼Ы─лla

Jamison Brereton

When the speech of reverence is set forth and the rite set forth, o men, in order to drink of the strengthening (soma),
drive here, o A┼Ыvins; come here. Seeking help, I call to you: provide
riches for the pious man.

Jamison Brereton Notes

On viv├бkс╣гaс╣Зa- see comm. ad VIII.45.11. Contra Geldner and Renou, I take it with тИЪvakс╣г тАШstrengthenтАЩ, not тИЪvac.

Griffith

When sacrifice which tells our reverence hath begun. Heroes! to drink the gushing juice,
Approach, ye Asvins, come to us: I call you, eager for your aid. Grant treasures to the worshipper.

Geldner

Bei der Huldigungsrede, bei der vorgesetzten Opfergabe, zum Trunke des redselig machenden Soma, ihr Herren, fahret hierher, Asvin, kommet her! Um euren Beistand bittend rufe ich euch, bringet dem Opfernden Kleinode!

Grassmann

O M├дnner, zu dem Opfermahl, zu trinken von dem schwellenden, Fahrt her o Ritter, kommt herbei, euch ruf’ ich h├╝lfsbegierig an, gebt Sch├дtze dem verehrenden.

Elizarenkova
